alternative: Sarah Elisabeth | id = U41740 | doi = 10.1093/ww/9780199540884.013.41740 }}&lt;/ref&gt; the younger of two daughters. alternative: Sir Denis | id = U152663 | type = was | volume = 2018 | edition = online}} {{subscription required}}&lt;/ref&gt; Having initially been cajoled by his parents to study medicine at the [[University of Glasgow]], he switched to an arts degree following a series of low marks in his examinations, graduating MA Hons. in 1923.&lt;ref name=Butterfield&gt;Herbert Butterfield, 'Denis Brogan', ''Encounter'', 1 April 1974.&lt;/ref&gt; Brogan subsequently studied at [[Balliol College, Oxford]], where he obtained a further degree in history in 1925. title: Tate's Cairn
alternative: 大老山}}'''Tate's Cairn''' ({{zh|c=大老山|cy=|l=Big Brother Mountain|s=|t=|p=}}) is a [[List of mountains, peaks and hills in Hong Kong|mountain]] in [[Hong Kong]] at {{Convert|583|m}} in height. It is one of the [[Eight Mountains of Kowloon|peaks of the Kowloon Ridge]] and falls within [[Ma On Shan Country Park]]. The peak began to appear on colonial maps in the 1860s but remained unnamed until the beginning of the 20th Century.&lt;ref&gt;{{Cite web|url=http://www.hkmaps.hk/mapviewer.html|title=HK Map Viewer|website=www.hkmaps.hk|access-date=2019-10-26}}&lt;/ref&gt;

title: Theodore Cressy Skeat
alternative: Theodore Cressy | id = U35048 | type = was | volume = 2019 | edition = online}} {{subscription required}}&lt;/ref&gt;&lt;ref&gt;'University News', ''Times'', 17 June 1929.&lt;/ref&gt; Following a further short spell as a student at the British School of Archaeology in Athens, he was recruited by the British Museum in 1931. His work coincided with two important acquisitions by the Trustees of the aforementioned institution, namely the ''[[Codex Sinaiticus]]'' and the apocryphal Gospel ''Egerton 2 Papyrus'' (a.k.a. the ''[[Egerton Gospel]]''). He made a name for himself with important contributions to [[palaeography]], papyrology, and codicology, particularly—but not only—in relation to these two acquisitions. He was the grandson of noted philologist [[Walter William Skeat]].

title: Pattini
alternative: Pattini Deviyo}}'''Pattini''' ({{Lang-si|පත්තිනි දෙවියෝ|lit=Pattiṉi Deviyō}}, {{Lang-ta|கண்ணகி அம்மன்|lit=Kaṇṇaki Am'man}},{{Lang-hi|पत्तिनी|lit=Devi Kannaki}}), is considered a guardian deity of Sri Lanka in [[Sri Lankan Buddhism]] and [[Sinhalese people|Sinhalese]] folklore. She is also worshipped by [[Hinduism in Sri Lanka|Sri Lankan Tamil Hindus]] by the name of ''[[Kannaki Amman]]''. She is considered the patron goddess of fertility and health, particularly protection against [[smallpox]], which is referred to as ''deviyange ledé'' ('the divine affliction') in the [[Sinhala language]].

title: Ma On Shan (peak)
alternative: 馬鞍山}}'''Ma On Shan''' ({{Zh|c=馬鞍山}}; literally: Saddle Peak) is a saddle-shaped peak in east of [[Tolo Harbour]] in the [[New Territories]] of [[Hong Kong]].  With a height of 702 metres (2,303&amp;nbsp;ft), it stands among the ten [[List of mountains, peaks and hills in Hong Kong|highest mountains in Hong Kong]].  The mountain borders [[Sha Tin District|Sha Tin]] and [[Tai Po District|Tai Po]] [[districts of Hong Kong|districts]].
